  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[
      function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){
        if (strx.indexOf("&lt;") != -1) {
          var s = strx.split("&lt;");
          for(var i=0; i&lt;s.length; i++) {
            if (s[i].indexOf("&gt;") != -1) {
              s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf("&gt;")+1,s[i].length);
            }
          }
          strx = s.join("");
        }
        chop = (chop &lt; strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2;
        while (strx.charAt(chop-1) != ' ' &amp;&amp; strx.indexOf(' ',chop) != -1) {
          chop++;
        }
        strx = strx.substring(0, chop - 1);
        return '&lt;div style="padding-bottom: 20px;"&gt;' + strx + ' ...&lt;/div&gt;';
      }
      
      function getFragment(srcId) {
        var srcDiv = document.getElementById(srcId);
        var src = srcDiv.innerHTML;
        //srcDiv.innerHTML = '';
        var elt = document.createElement('div');
        elt.innerHTML = src.replace(/ src=/gi, ' _src=');
        return elt;
      }
      
      function rewriteBlogspotUrl(imgTag, newSize) {
        if (newSize === undefined) {
          newSize = '400';
        }
        if (imgTag.hasAttribute('height') &amp;&amp; imgTag.hasAttribute('width')) {
          var height = imgTag.getAttribute('height');
          var width = imgTag.getAttribute('width');
          if (height &gt; width) {
            var s = Math.ceil(parseInt(newSize) * height / width / 100);
            newSize = (s * 100).toString();
          }
        }
        if (/.*.bp.blogspot.com/.test(imgTag.getAttribute('_src'))) {
          var originalImageSrc = imgTag.getAttribute('_src');
          var newImageSrc = originalImageSrc.replace(
              /\/s\d+\//, '/s' + newSize + '/');
          return newImageSrc;
        }
      }
      
      function getThumbnail(fragment) {
        var imgs = fragment.getElementsByTagName('img');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; imgs.length; i++) {
          newImageSrc = rewriteBlogspotUrl(imgs[i]);
          if (newImageSrc !== undefined) {
            return newImageSrc;
          }
        }
        return '';
      }
      
      function getSummary(fragment, length) {
        var maxLength = length || 251;
        var summary = fragment.textContent || fragment.innerText;
        summary.replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
        if (summary.length &lt; maxLength) {
          return summary;
        } else {
          var nextSpace = summary.indexOf(' ', maxLength - 3)
          return summary.substring(0, nextSpace) + ' ...';
        }
      }
      
      function createMetaTag(property, content) {
        var meta = document.createElement('meta');
        meta.setAttribute('property', property);
        meta.setAttribute('content', content);
        return meta;
      }
      
      function addDescriptionMeta(srcId, summaryLength) {
        var length = summaryLength || 80;
        var dest = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var fragment = getFragment(srcId);
        var summary = getSummary(fragment, length).trim();
        dest.appendChild(createMetaTag('og:description', summary));
      }
      
      function createPostPreview(srcId, destId, postUrl) {
        var div = document.getElementById(destId);
        var fragment = getFragment(srcId);
        var thumbnailUrl = getThumbnail(fragment);
        if (thumbnailUrl.length &gt; 0) {
          var img = document.createElement('img');
          img.setAttribute('src', getThumbnail(fragment));
          img.setAttribute('width', '300px')
          var ref = document.createElement('a');
          ref.setAttribute('href', postUrl);
          ref.appendChild(img)
          var innerDiv = document.createElement('div');
          innerDiv.setAttribute('class', 'crop');
          innerDiv.appendChild(ref);
          div.appendChild(innerDiv);
        }
        var innerSpan = document.createElement('span');
        innerSpan.setAttribute('id', 'read-more-link');
        innerSpan.innerHTML = 'Read more ...';
        var innerDiv = document.createElement('div');
        innerDiv.setAttribute('id', 'read-more');
        innerDiv.appendChild(innerSpan);
        var ref = document.createElement('a');
        ref.setAttribute('href', postUrl);
        ref.innerHTML = getSummary(fragment);
        ref.appendChild(innerDiv);
        var summaryDiv = document.createElement('div');
        summaryDiv.setAttribute('class', 'posting');
        summaryDiv.appendChild(ref);
        div.appendChild(summaryDiv);
      }
      
      function createPostPreviewOriginal(srcId, destId, postUrl) {
        var div = document.getElementById(destId);
        var fragment = getFragment(srcId);
        var thumbnailUrl = getThumbnail(fragment);
        if (thumbnailUrl.length &gt; 0) {
          var divContent = '&lt;div class="crop"&gt;&lt;a href="' + postUrl + '"&gt;';
          divContent += '&lt;img src="' + getThumbnail(fragment) + '" width="300px;" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
          div.innerHTML = divContent;
        }
        var summaryDiv = '&lt;div class="posting"&gt;&lt;a href="' + postUrl + '"&gt;';
        summaryDiv += getSummary(fragment);
        summaryDiv += '&lt;div id="read-more" class="read-more"&gt;&lt;span id="read-more-link"&gt;';
        summaryDiv += 'Read more ...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
        div.innerHTML += summaryDiv;
      }
      
      function resizeImages(postTitle, srcId, destId) {
        var div = document.getElementById(destId);
        var fragment = getFragment(srcId);
        var imgs = fragment.getElementsByTagName('img');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; imgs.length; i++) {
          var width = '000';
          if (imgs[i].hasAttribute('width')) {
            var w = Math.ceil(imgs[i].getAttribute('width') * 1.3 / 100);
            width = (w * 100).toString();
          }
          var newImgSrc = (rewriteBlogspotUrl(imgs[i], width) ||
                           imgs[i].getAttribute('_src'));
          imgs[i].setAttribute('src', newImgSrc);
          imgs[i].removeAttribute('_src');
          imgs[i].setAttribute('alt', postTitle + ' from Fun at Home with Kids');
        };
        var embeds = fragment.getElementsByTagName('embed');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; embeds.length; i++) {
          embeds[i].setAttribute('src', embeds[i].getAttribute('_src'))
          embeds[i].removeAttribute('_src');
        }
        div.innerHTML = fragment.innerHTML;
      }
      
      function addTitleMeta() {
        var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var title = document.getElementsByTagName('title')[0];
        head.appendChild(createMetaTag('og:title', title.innerHTML.trim()));
      }
      
      function addAuthorMeta(author) {
        var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        head.appendChild(createMetaTag('og:author', author));
      }
      
      function addUrlMeta(url) {
        var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        head.appendChild(createMetaTag('og:url', url));
      }
      
      function addImgMeta(divId, maxTags) {
        var numTags = maxTags || 6;
        var div = document.getElementById(divId);
        var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var imgs = div.getElementsByTagName('img');
        var totalTags = Math.min(numTags, imgs.length)
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; totalTags; i++) {
          imgs[i].setAttribute('itemprop', 'image');
          head.appendChild(createMetaTag('og:image', imgs[i].getAttribute('src')));
        };
      }
      
      function addAltTags(postTitle, divId) {
        var div = document.getElementById(divId);
        var imgs = div.getElementsByTagName('img');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; imgs.length; i++) {
          if (!imgs[i].hasAttribute('alt')) {
            imgs[i].setAttribute('alt', postTitle + ' from Fun at Home with Kids');
          }
        };
      }

      </h1>
      <h2 id="blog-desc">

       </span>
      </h2>

             <li style="display: none;">
              Simple Small Worlds:  Fizzing Hidden Ocean World
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="title">
            <a name="8231280163253014216">
            </a>
            <h2>
             <div class="post-display-title">
              <a href="http://www.funathomewithkids.com/2013/03/simple-small-worlds-fizzing-hidden.html" rel="bookmark" title="Simple Small Worlds:  Fizzing Hidden Ocean World">
               <span class="entry-title" itemprop="name">
                <span itemprop="description">
                 Simple Small Worlds:  Fizzing Hidden Ocean World
                </span>
               </span>
              </a>
             </div>
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="data">
            <span class="author">
             By
             <a href="https://plus.google.com/110728339748546909210?rel=author">
              <span itemprop="author">
               Asia Citro
              </span>
              <script type="text/javascript">
               addAuthorMeta("Asia Citro");
              </script>
             </a>
            </span>
            <span class="clock" itemprop="datePublished">
             Saturday, March 23, 2013
            </span>
            <div class="copyright-text">
              2014 Asia Citro
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="pagepost">
            <p>
            </p>
            <div class="cover">
             <div id="bodyContainer-8231280163253014216">
              <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <i>
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/" rel="nofollow" style="font-family: inherit;" target="_blank">
                  Safari Ltd
                 </a>
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  sent us a TOOB free of charge at my request. My review of their products is not swayed by this as I already loved them!
                 </span>
                </i>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 One of the most classic subjects for a small world is the ocean. Full of amazing, interesting, and often cute creatures - oceans are full of wonder for toddlers and preschoolers. An ocean is a great setting for some small world imaginative play! When I think of oceans, I think of sand, shells, and beautiful blue water. Rather than just fill a tub with blue water, though, I wanted to come up with something a little more creative. To stay true to my goal with my Simple Small Worlds series, I wanted to keep prep and materials to a minimum.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit; margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                </span>
                <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zvqJItx2yno/UU0gPW7RbNI/AAAAAAACCPk/a1tr3OnDuBc/s1600/IMG_7836.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <img border="0" height="372" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zvqJItx2yno/UU0gPW7RbNI/AAAAAAACCPk/a1tr3OnDuBc/s1600/IMG_7836.JPG" width="640"/>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <i>
                 This post contains affiliate links for your convenience.
                </i>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 We had SO much fun with our
                 <a href="http://www.funathomewithkids.com/2013/02/help-leprechaun-find-his-gold-day-two.html">
                  fizzing treasure rocks
                 </a>
                 during our
                 <a href="http://www.funathomewithkids.com/2013/02/help-leprechaun-find-his-gold-older.html">
                  Find the Leprechaun's Gold Hunt
                 </a>
                 - it gave me the idea to make some baking soda dough and shape it like shells around several of the
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/collection/collectionproductlist?collection_id=1&amp;group_id=1&amp;productid=695104" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Ocean TOOB creatures
                 </a>
                 .
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 I promise that this is SUPER easy. Really. In fact, I did it in less than five minutes as I was needing to pick S up from preschool! You will need to make the dough/baking soda shells a day in advance, though, to give them time to dry and harden. That's the only hard part!
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 To make baking soda dough, you just need baking soda and water. I used two boxes of baking soda to make six shells.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UHoh6JBVnYo/UU0jA5lfZPI/AAAAAAACCQE/NnQ0waOkH-I/s1600/IMG_7539.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UHoh6JBVnYo/UU0jA5lfZPI/AAAAAAACCQE/NnQ0waOkH-I/s1600/IMG_7539.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 Once you've emptied the baking soda into the bowl, add just enough water that the dough is crumbly. Err on the side of too little water. Here I could have actually done a little less - so think of the below picture as showing you the maximum amount of water to add. :)
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-J1DDSaPymm4/UU0jAzNwmSI/AAAAAAACCQI/0iNiTv0bF5w/s1600/IMG_7541.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-J1DDSaPymm4/UU0jAzNwmSI/AAAAAAACCQI/0iNiTv0bF5w/s1600/IMG_7541.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 After that, I took six of the
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/collection/collectionproductlist?collection_id=1&amp;group_id=1&amp;productid=695104" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Ocean TOOB
                 </a>
                 figures and using a shell as a reference point, made the general shape of a shell by hand (this took about 15 seconds per "shell") and then placed the shells on a sheet of wax paper. After making the shape, I used the back of a real shell to make some grooves like the shells I was planning to use in the small world. Like I said, the whole thing took less than five minutes - I happened to be watching a clock. I hope a lot of you will give these a try because they are just so much fun.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UOYSUPRFlXw/UU0gKIg0vNI/AAAAAAACCNs/h94SfWuPz5Q/s1600/IMG_7690.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="344" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UOYSUPRFlXw/UU0gKIg0vNI/AAAAAAACCNs/h94SfWuPz5Q/s1600/IMG_7690.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 One of my favorite things about the
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/collection/collectionproductlist?collection_id=1&amp;group_id=1" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Safari Ltd TOOBS
                 </a>
                 is that they have natural groupings that lend themselves to both cohesive small world play and to learning about different groups of animals. I knew that the
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/collection/collectionproductlist?collection_id=1&amp;group_id=1&amp;productid=695104" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Ocean TOOB
                 </a>
                 would include a
                 <span style="background-color: white;">
                  sea lion, eagle ray, starfish, two turtles, penguin, octopus, moray eel, humpback whale, sperm whale, hammerhead shark, tiger shark, and a dolphin - so I headed to the library last weekend and picked up a variety of both fiction and non-fiction books on those animals. When she saw the small world, S was able to identify a few of the animals because of the reading we'd done, which was pretty cool!
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Facch0OLnRY/UU0gRCrmuFI/AAAAAAACCP0/F6AB-JXJTKM/s1600/IMG_7397.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="336" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Facch0OLnRY/UU0gRCrmuFI/AAAAAAACCP0/F6AB-JXJTKM/s1600/IMG_7397.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 So for the set-up, I set out our
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/search?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;index=aps&amp;keywords=oilcloth%20by%20the%20yard&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;tag=cracit06-20" target="_blank">
                  splat mat
                 </a>
                 <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=cracit06-20&amp;l=ur2&amp;o=1" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" width="1"/>
                 and filled our plastic storage bin with the now dry baking soda shells, several different
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/search?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;index=aps&amp;keywords=shells&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;tag=cracit06-20" target="_blank">
                  shells,
                 </a>
                 <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=cracit06-20&amp;l=ur2&amp;o=1" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" width="1"/>
                 the
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/search?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;index=aps&amp;keywords=decorative%20gems&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;tag=cracit06-20" target="_blank">
                  glass gems
                 </a>
                 <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=cracit06-20&amp;l=ur2&amp;o=1" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" width="1"/>
                 I used in Frog World (we found ours at the Dollar Store), and the remaining
                 <a href="http://safariltd.us/collection/collectionproductlist?collection_id=1&amp;group_id=1&amp;productid=695104" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Ocean TOOB
                 </a>
                 animals.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-l1HDe677IzU/UU0gLQZHEfI/AAAAAAACCOE/k4C_rnDf_TM/s1600/IMG_7699.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-l1HDe677IzU/UU0gLQZHEfI/AAAAAAACCOE/k4C_rnDf_TM/s1600/IMG_7699.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 S was already so excited that she sat down to play for a few minutes before she realized - "wait, Mama, where's the water? Shouldn't there be water in the ocean?"
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PWhxkHM2_bw/UU0gKf2eLnI/AAAAAAACCN0/x-1eHRfSnLI/s1600/IMG_7693.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="342" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PWhxkHM2_bw/UU0gKf2eLnI/AAAAAAACCN0/x-1eHRfSnLI/s1600/IMG_7693.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 To get the "ocean" started, I provided her with four squeeze bottles full of blue vinegar. I used four drops of blue food coloring per bottle, though you could absolutely use liquid watercolors. In fact, I would have used
                </span>
                <a href="http://www.jdoqocy.com/click-7226120-10651292?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.discountschoolsupply.com%2FProduct%2FProductDetail.aspx%3Fproduct%3D16821&amp;cjsku=16821" onmouseout="window.status=' ';return true;" onmouseover="window.status='http://www.discountschoolsupply.com';return true;" target="_blank">
                 Colorations Liquid Watercolors
                </a>
                ,
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 only our blue (from the tropical series) is really more of a green-blue, and I had my heart set on a bright blue ocean. :)
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-F39gmM4Soos/UU0gLm1OETI/AAAAAAACCOM/gwKO_0GuZBA/s1600/IMG_7700.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-F39gmM4Soos/UU0gLm1OETI/AAAAAAACCOM/gwKO_0GuZBA/s1600/IMG_7700.JPG" width="582"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 I instructed her to use the squirt bottles on the white shells to see what happened. She gleefully went to work dissolving the first shell...which revealed a turtle!
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zvEMiulelPo/UU0gLj0ZM2I/AAAAAAACCOQ/46pVx6E44tM/s1600/IMG_7718.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zvEMiulelPo/UU0gLj0ZM2I/AAAAAAACCOQ/46pVx6E44tM/s1600/IMG_7718.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ABuwmKoVAXk/UU0gLyg9IuI/AAAAAAACCOU/2n1RGwSz5KE/s1600/IMG_7721.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ABuwmKoVAXk/UU0gLyg9IuI/AAAAAAACCOU/2n1RGwSz5KE/s1600/IMG_7721.JPG" width="426"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 After removing each animal, she loved squirting more vinegar to watch them fizz and "to clean them off".
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-meY39fRMybg/UU0gMT3UXlI/AAAAAAACCOc/aZy-I5bcVW8/s1600/IMG_7727.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="468" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-meY39fRMybg/UU0gMT3UXlI/AAAAAAACCOc/aZy-I5bcVW8/s1600/IMG_7727.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 Moving on to the next shell!
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HQj6zntQ-Fo/UU0gMqeypAI/AAAAAAACCOk/lPr-FZF6epE/s1600/IMG_7741.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HQj6zntQ-Fo/UU0gMqeypAI/AAAAAAACCOk/lPr-FZF6epE/s1600/IMG_7741.JPG" width="446"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 "A cute little penguin, Mama!"
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6ted5TcqxUg/UU0gMwfKp3I/AAAAAAACCOs/dgDH-jhMhxQ/s1600/IMG_7747.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6ted5TcqxUg/UU0gMwfKp3I/AAAAAAACCOs/dgDH-jhMhxQ/s1600/IMG_7747.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 This one had the best reveal! The octopus' eyes peeking out as its shell dissolved were cracking me up.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UWaf9t_3150/UU0gNFn0F9I/AAAAAAACCO0/tq2Q1Tv2fEw/s1600/IMG_7767.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UWaf9t_3150/UU0gNFn0F9I/AAAAAAACCO0/tq2Q1Tv2fEw/s1600/IMG_7767.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 "Ooh! Mama! A ray!" Once S was finished finding all the hidden creatures, I added several containers of water from our sink to make the "ocean" a bit deeper.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ejHvs-h4bTk/UU0gNdZZw4I/AAAAAAACCO4/Vjbx05xa1Wg/s1600/IMG_7796.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ejHvs-h4bTk/UU0gNdZZw4I/AAAAAAACCO4/Vjbx05xa1Wg/s1600/IMG_7796.JPG" width="426"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 After all the shells were dissolved, the baking soda doubled as "white sand" at the bottom of her ocean world. She smoothed out the "sand" and kept commenting on how soft it was. I couldn't resist playing in it myself, and she was right! The baking soda is silky smooth at the bottom. We could even write and make designs in it, which was fun.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mYWfhpyPKwQ/UU0gN7d-XCI/AAAAAAACCPA/dQxKonzu8rI/s1600/IMG_7817.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mYWfhpyPKwQ/UU0gN7d-XCI/AAAAAAACCPA/dQxKonzu8rI/s1600/IMG_7817.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 S found out that adding some of the residual vinegar in the squeeze bottles would still make little foamy eruptions, so she used every last drop of the blue vinegar. :)
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LV3YwvZya3U/UU0gNSDRI4I/AAAAAAACCPI/msxTQsaW7uU/s1600/IMG_7813.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="420" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LV3YwvZya3U/UU0gNSDRI4I/AAAAAAACCPI/msxTQsaW7uU/s1600/IMG_7813.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 Here S was helping the whale swim over to his friends on the other side of the ocean.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zUGQLdULiK4/UU0gPjFdLiI/AAAAAAACCPg/QEadCIJEEqo/s1600/IMG_7852.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zUGQLdULiK4/UU0gPjFdLiI/AAAAAAACCPg/QEadCIJEEqo/s1600/IMG_7852.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                 We had so much fun with this world! S played with it for almost 3 hours and declared it "the best project you've ever thought of, Mama!"
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-URzK4LMJt2E/UsT0bVr5KFI/AAAAAAAC--o/V_lJdEN4VTw/s1600/PicMonkey+Collage+(35).jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-URzK4LMJt2E/UsT0bVr5KFI/AAAAAAAC--o/V_lJdEN4VTw/s1600/PicMonkey+Collage+(35).jpg" width="320"/>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                <br/>
               </div>

                           Awesome!  I am trying to use common things and/or repeat elements in the Simple Small worlds so hopefully that happens more and more often.  :)  And I think the girls will love the ocean world - it's SO fun!!!
                          </p>

                          <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_82MC">
                           Hi Valerie!  We do that with Easter eggs, too!  Miniatures last so much longer than candy.  :)  We just do 2 yards of oilcloth (as opposed to a finished splat mat).  Works fabulously!  Before that we did a waterproof disposable tablecloth, but that wore through more quickly.  The oilcloth is SUPER strong and hardy.  :)
                          </p>

                          <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_157MC">
                           Hi Karen!  YES, start them ASAP.  They ideally need about 24 hours to dry, but get them as close as you can.  If you make them right now and they sit out overnight they should be pretty hardy.  They'll be more hardy after a full 24, but just move them gently tomorrow for the party and it shouldn't be a problem.  Good luck and happy birthday to your daughter!
                          </p>
